< review>
I am a returning customer for Diamond Shine Hand Car Wash and Detail. My car was a disaster. I own a 2016 Honda Civic with tan colored soft seats and I own a dog. When I take my dog to the dog park, she's rolling around in the mud and dirt and she comes back to the back seat of my car with slobber all over my seats. So imagine this collecting and building up in the past 6-8 months.

I called Diamond Shine and the owner scheduled me for a Saturday drop off. My appointment was scheduled at 12:00pm but because I had a lot of errands to do, I asked if I can drop it off earlier and leave the keys with them. They told me that they preferred to do that and let me know that I can drop it off anytime before then.

I dropped off my car 30 minutes after they opened on a Saturday. I walked with the owner to my car to see the condition of my car - the interior was a mess. I have tan seats and there was dirt and stains all over. Really wishing I had leather seats at this point. It was nearly embarrassing. We discussed a quote and it was more than reasonable. A diamond package was done and they hooked it up with a nice and unexpected discount because I was a returning customer!

The car was with them for nearly the whole day, which was fine because I had another car I was using. When I came to pick up my car at the end of the day, I almost could not recognize it. The people who detailed the car showed me what they worked on and it was spotless. There was a deep scratch on the side of my car from when my car scraped against some unknown object and that scratch was noticeable (it was white) and that would not come off, and even a previous detail place informed me that it cannot be come off. I gave up trying to get that scratch off.  That scratch was on the left back side of the car near where the handles were.  But Diamond Shine manage to work their magic and you cannot see the scratch at all. Wow. The amount of appreciation and gratefulness I have for the amazing service for both to me and my car, the positive attitudes elicited from everyone that worked there, and the great job done to my mess of a car for a very great price. I'm still in awe.

Thank you Diamond Shine. You have scored yourself a loyal customer. For those who are waiting and questioning, please go to them and just talk to the owner in person to discuss your options and ask questions. They will not force you to buy a package that you do not want, it is totally customer at will, compare to other detail places that will always try to make you pay for the highest package. In this case, I chose to do the highest package because my car needed it. Last time I chose a silver package, and my car was still returned in great condition. Cannot express my gratitude enough. Thank you!< /review>

< text>
I've had the worst experience with this fish store. Let me start off by saying I am an experienced fish keeper and know all about the nitrogen cycle and quarantining fish. I purchased 11 fish for a grand total of $40. I got home and floated the fish for 2 hours before releasing them into the quarantine tank. Straight out the bag 2 fish looked like they were on their way out, immediate sign of unhealthy fish. Its been 3 days since Ive purchased these fish and I have lost 5 fish so far. At this point I'm not too confident the rest will survive. I have purchased other fish from different fish stores, that have been quarantined longer than the fish from The Reef, and I have not lost any of their fish and its been weeks. I definitely advise everyone to handpick their fish as the woman who helped me acted like it was her first day on the job. She had a hard time catching the fish and most likely hurt them in the process. Also go figure, they only have a 24 hour exchange window. I will not be purchasing any fish from them anymore, I will update this post as the days go on in case I lose more fish from them.</text>

< review>
Ate here for the first time tonight-- service and food both excellent. Tiny indoors, about 8-10 tables, but also tables on the patio out front. Four of us, had spaghetti & meatballs, two mini-pizzas, and Caesar salad w/parmesan chicken. Everything was pronounced quite tasty and fresh. Service was friendly and fairly fast. They also deliver, which we will definitely take advantage of in future. A nice neighborhood discovery!</review>

' WOW'
I  recently had the urge for a Big Mac.  I drove to this location.  Parking was OK.  It was around 2 PM.  I had problems communicating with he cashier.  I ordered 2 Big Mac's no salt.  She repeats back to me OK no sauce.  I repeat no salt and and then I said no sal.  OK OK, she says and repeats back to me 4 Big Macs no sal.  I held up two fingers and repeated back to her 2 Big Mac's no salt.  She repeats back to me holding up 4 fingers saying, four Big Macs no sauce.  Wow.  We finally got that straightened out, however the line behind me had grown and the customers were upset.  Sh rang me up and I was surprised at the cost.  Expensive.

While I waited to the side of the counter I saw such congestion due to the fact that the Self order kiosk was located where the line would start at the counter.  People and kids bumping into each other.  Not a good location for the kiosk, breaks the flow.

Meanwhile as I stood to the side waiting for my order to go, I had observed grouchy stressed customers as they entered, while they ordered and when they received their messed up orders.  Honestly, it was quite a show.  There was bad ju ju in this place.  I stayed close to the door.

I make it a habit to check my order before leaving an establishment.  THIS time I didn't, I wanted to get out and get home.  Upon my arrival I was surprised at the size of the BIG Mac,  they looked like sliders (mini hamburgers), more bread than anything.  For the price they charged I had expected more.< /review>
